	var purl = window.location.href;
	var url = '//ads.pubmatic.com/AdServer/js/pwt/159924/3565';
	var profileVersionId = '';
	if(purl.indexOf('pwtv=')>0){
		var regexp = /pwtv=(.*?)(&|$)/g;
		var matches = regexp.exec(purl);
		if(matches.length >= 2 && matches[1].length > 0){
			profileVersionId = '/'+matches[1];
		}
	}
	var wtads = document.createElement('script');
	wtads.async = true;
	wtads.type = 'text/javascript';
	wtads.src = url+profileVersionId+'/pwt.js';
	var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
	node.parentNode.insertBefore(wtads, node);
})();

 }
 placeTag.parentNode.insertBefore(scriptTag, placeTag);

<script type="text/javascript">
googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
          googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
      //Pulling the ad sizes from URL for testing the ad sizes 
  function test_check(){
    if (window.location.href.indexOf("test") >= 0) {
      var vars = window.location.href.split('?');
      for (i in vars){
        if (vars[i].indexOf("test") >= 0){
          return [vars[i].split('=')[1]]
        }
      }}
    return [""]
  }
  // GET Cookie code for making ad targeting easier
  var reRegExpChar = /[\\^$.*+?()[\]{}|]/g,
  reHasRegExpChar = RegExp(reRegExpChar.source);
  function escapeRegExp(string) {
    return string && reHasRegExpChar.test(string) ? string.replace(reRegExpChar, '\\$&') : string;
  }
  function getCookie(name) {
    var k = escapeRegExp(name);
    var v = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + k + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return v ? v[2] : null;
  }
  function initRecentlyViewedTracking() {
    // Get recently viewed cookie and populate data variables
    var recentlyViewedCookie = getCookie('recentlyViewedList');
    if (recentlyViewedCookie && recentlyViewedCookie !== 'false') {
      var recentlyViewedCookieArray = recentlyViewedCookie.split(',').reverse();
      return recentlyViewedCookieArray;
    }
    else {
      return '';
    }
  }
  setTimeout(function () {
    if (typeof drupalSettings != "undefined") {
      var uid = drupalSettings.user.uid;
      var watchlist_symbols = {
          "async": false,
          "crossDomain": true,
          "url": "/api/v1/watchlist/" + uid,
          "method": "GET",
          "headers": {
          "content-Type" : "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        }
      }
      if (uid != 0) { // User is signed in and has ID, pass Watchlist Symbols and Any Tipranks portfolio personal info to target
        window.jQuery.ajax(watchlist_symbols).then(function(responseText) {
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_watchlist_symbol_list", responseText.watchlist);
        });
        var portfolioProfessionCookie = getCookie('portfolioProfession');
        var portfolioAnnualIncomeCookie = getCookie('portfolioAnnualIncome');
        var portfolioAgeCookie = getCookie('portfolioAge');
        if (portfolioProfessionCookie) {
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_portfolio_profession", portfolioProfessionCookie);
        }
        if (portfolioAnnualIncomeCookie) {
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_portfolio_annual_income", portfolioAnnualIncomeCookie);
        }
        if (portfolioAgeCookie) {
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_portfolio_age", portfolioAgeCookie);
        }
      }
    }
  }, 2000);
  googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_page_instance_id", digitalData.pageInstanceID || '');
  googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_page_template", digitalData.page.category.pageType || '');
  googletag.pubads().setTargeting("nasdaqdotcom_publisher", digitalData.page.pageInfo.publisher || '');
